See for yourself by <a href="https://www.investing.com/pro/deep-link?view=marketing-pro-street-insider&amp;entry=pro_recap&amp;sub_entry=3075314&amp;category=tech_w&amp;utm_term=pro_recap&amp;utm_content=3075314" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:starting a 7-day free trial;elm:context_link;itc:0" class="link ">starting a 7-day free trial</a>.</p><h2><strong>Apple comes out ahead</strong></h2><p>On Thursday Apple Inc (NASDAQ:AAPL) topped first-quarter estimates with earnings per share of $1.54 vs. the $1.43 average analyst estimate, driven by stronger-than-expected iPhone sales.</p><p>Apple also boosted its dividend and announced a $90 billion share buyback program.</p><p>Goldman Sachs raised the price target to $209 per share on Buy-rated AAPL stock after &quot;strong&quot; results:</p><p>&quot;We gain confidence in our Buy rating and believe AAPL shares continue to be attractive.&quot;</p><p>KeyBanc also hiked the price target, to $180 per share from the prior $177, noting that Emerging Markets strength a the tech giant offloaded weaker U.S. results.</p><p>Shares were up more than 2% for the week.</p><h2><strong>AMD&#39;s roller coaster week</strong></h2><p>Advanced Micro Devices (NASDAQ:AMD) reported a better-than-expected Q1 on Tuesday but issued disappointing guidance, triggering a 9% selloff in the shares in the next session.</p><p>BofA cut the stock to Neutral from Buy, citing a &quot;range of headwinds&quot; including &quot;aggressive pricing/promotion pressure from main rival Intel (NASDAQ:INTC).&quot;</p><p>Citi, for its part, raised the price target on AMD stock to $85 per share, and BMO highlighted the company&#39;s continued market share gains against Intel.</p><p>Then, on Thursday afternoon, shares clawed most of their way back following a story from Bloomberg that said Microsoft (NASDAQ:MSFT) is helping finance AMDs expansion into AI chips.</p><p>Microsoft and AMD have teamed to create an alternative to Nvidia (NASDAQ:NVDA) processors for artificial intelligence, the report said, citing people with knowledge of the matter. Microsoft will provide financial support to bolster AMDs efforts, as it works with the chipmaker on a homegrown Microsoft processor for AI workloads.</p><div class="caas-readmore caas-readmore-collapse"><button class="link caas-button collapse-button" aria-label="" title="" data-ylk="elm:readmore;slk:Story continues">Story continues</button></div><p>Through it all, <a href="https://www.investing.com/pro/deep-link?view=marketing-pro-street-insider&amp;entry=pro_recap&amp;sub_entry=3075314&amp;category=tech_w&amp;utm_term=pro_recap&amp;utm_content=3075314" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:InvestingPro;elm:context_link;itc:0" class="link ">InvestingPro</a> shot these updates to subscribers at breakneck speed. <a href="https://www.investing.com/pro/deep-link?view=marketing-pro-street-insider&amp;entry=pro_recap&amp;sub_entry=3075314&amp;category=tech_w&amp;utm_term=pro_recap&amp;utm_content=3075314" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:Never miss another tech headline again;elm:context_link;itc:0" class="link ">Never miss another tech headline again</a>.</p><p>AMD shares were ultimately off about 1% for the week.</p><h2><strong>Qualcomm&#39;s weak guidance</strong></h2><p>Qualcomm (NASDAQ:QCOM) shares slid after the company forecasted far lower-than-anticipated results for is fiscal third quarter: The company expects 3Q23 EPS in the range of $1.70-$1.90, compared with the consensus of $2.20, and revenue in the range of $8.1-8.9B, compared to the consensus of $9.25B.</p><div class="caas-da"><div id="sda-INARTICLE"></div></div><p>Q2 earnings of $2.15 per share were in line with expectations.</p><p>The company said demand for smartphones had deteriorated as China remains weak, calling the macroeconomic environment &quot;challenging.&quot;</p><p>Mizuho cut the price target by $10 to $140. As <a href="https://www.investing.com/pro/deep-link?view=marketing-pro-street-insider&amp;entry=pro_recap&amp;sub_entry=3075314&amp;category=tech_w&amp;utm_term=pro_recap&amp;utm_content=3075314" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:InvestingPro;elm:context_link;itc:0" class="link ">InvestingPro</a> reported in real time, Deutsche Bank cut the company&#39;s price target to $130 from the prior $150 while maintaining its Buy rating.</p><p>Deutsche called the guidance &quot;disappointing by any measure&quot; but also believes the company &quot;should be an attractive beneficiary of the eventual cyclical rebound once one actually occurs (not a matter of if, but rather when).&quot;</p><p>Shares sank more than 7% for the week.</p><h2><strong>Block&#39;s robust Q1</strong></h2><p>Block (NYSE:SQ) shares initially bumped higher after the fintech name reported better-than-expected Q1 results: earnings per share of $0.40 vs. Wall Street&#39;s estimate of $0.35, and above-par revenue of $4.99 billion.</p><p>For the full year, the company raised its full-year adjusted EBITDA (earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, and amortization) forecast to $1.36 billion, up from the prior $1.3B.</p><p>Morgan Stanley and JPMorgan were both positive on the stock after earnings. JPMorgan sees more room for further upside, calling its operating leverage potential &quot;underappreciated by the market.&quot; It added, &quot;SQ remains one of our favorite ideas.&quot;</p><p>For the week, though, shares slipped 2.5%.</p><h2><strong>Coinbase ekes out a beat</strong></h2><p>Coinbase&#39;s Q1 results were better than feared, driven by cost cuts and a jump in subscription revenue: The company lost just $0.34 per share, far better than expectations for $1.39 in the red.</p><p>After its Thursday report, shares were trading about 9% higher.</p><p>Looking ahead, the company said it expected subscription and services revenue to fall in the second quarter. For the full year it continues to seek to improve full-year 2023 adjusted EBITDA in absolute dollar terms versus full-year 2022.</p><p>BofA said the results were solid but that big fundamental questions remain unanswered about the company, and maintained its Underperform rating on Coinbase (NASDAQ:COIN): &quot;We continue to think retail crypto volumes will remain weak and the regulatory overhang will linger for some time,&quot; the analyst said in a note.</p><p>Barclays lowered the price target to $61 from $74 per share. The analyst highlighted an uplift in retail take rate, while also noting that this trend may not prove to be sustainable.</p><p>Amid turbulent markets and a firehose of headlines, <a href="https://www.investing.com/pro/deep-link?view=marketing-pro-street-insider&amp;entry=pro_recap&amp;sub_entry=3075314&amp;category=tech_w&amp;utm_term=pro_recap&amp;utm_content=3075314" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:rapidly seize on the most important ones;elm:context_link;itc:0" class="link ">rapidly seize on the most important ones</a> to fatten your
